Suspicion Regarding Fire in Machine Factory Upstairs

Accidental Fire or Arson?

Whose Responsibility Is It?

Wu Lianqing, the owner of the Wu Hua Chang Machine Factory on Peng Road, rented the upstairs side room of the factory to Liu Wenrui, who lived there with his family. Wu's family lived in the main hall upstairs. Around the end of last year, a fire broke out in Liu's room, also causing damage to Wu's property. After the fire was extinguished by the fire brigade, the police discovered many suspicious points, and both households had substantial insurance policies, suggesting arson for compensation. Liu and Wu were arrested and brought to the Provisional Court for repeated questioning. Examining Magistrate Tan Xinzhen personally inspected the fire scene. Yesterday morning, witnesses were summoned again for further debate. According to the testimony of Zhou's wife, Wu was indeed at her house eating New Year's Eve dinner and playing mahjong on the night of the fire and did not return home. Wu's wife, Liu, testified that Liu Wenrui woke her up, and she immediately got out of bed and saw the door curtain on fire. She tore the curtain down, retreated, and then ran downstairs, escaping through the back door. Judge Tan then ordered the debate to begin, stating that the scope of the debate would focus on whether the fire, which started in Liu's room, was accidental or arson, and if it was arson, whether it was done by Liu alone or in collusion with Wu, and who bore the responsibility. The three lawyers representing the two defendants then presented their arguments, followed by a response from the police lawyer. After the debate, the defendants' lawyer requested that Wu be released on bail pending judgment. Judge Tan then ordered Liu Wenrui to be remanded in custody and Wu Lianqing to be released on bail upon payment of 4,000 yuan in cash and 4,000 yuan in the form of a shop. The date for sentencing was set for the morning of March 24.

Who Kidnapped Ji Saizhen?

Neighbors All Say He A'san Took Her Out to Play

Ji Dagouzi, a Fuying native residing in a straw hut without a number plate in the Zhabei Zhonghua Xin, worked as a rickshaw puller. His wife, Zhou, worked in a silk factory peeling cocoons. Both were middle-aged and had a nine-year-old daughter named Saizhen, whom they cherished greatly. Ji went out to pull the rickshaw every day until the following morning when he handed over the shift. His wife went to work at the factory during the day, leaving Saizhen at home. Ji had a fellow villager, He A'san, living in Lan Ni Du, Pudong, who had visited Ji a few days ago and left in the evening. Unexpectedly, Saizhen suddenly disappeared yesterday. After inquiring with neighboring children, they said that Saizhen was playing in front of the door and was taken away by the person who had come before, saying that they were going out to play. Upon hearing this, Ji concluded that He had kidnapped her but did not know where he lived in Lan Ni Du. He had to cross the river to Pudong to search, and at the same time reported the incident to the police district for arrest.

North China Freight Rates to Increase

All shipping companies in Shanghai have agreed to increase freight rates for goods shipped from Shanghai to the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River and to Southeast Asia by 15% and 10% respectively, starting next week. As for the route to North China, the Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and China Merchants companies have also agreed that starting from April 1, all goods transported from Shanghai to Tianjin and other ports will increase by 10%, except for piece goods and flour, which will remain at the original price. This has already been announced to all customs brokers and businesses.

Preparatory Committee Meeting of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions

The 26th Meeting

The Shanghai Special Municipal Federation of Trade Unions held its 26th preparatory committee meeting yesterday. Present were Gu Yongquan, Zhang Yaoming, Xu Shaochuan, Ge Hecai, Tang Junsheng, Zhou Zixiang, Chairman Lu Jingshi, and recorder Liu Yunqian. After the customary formalities and report, the following matters were discussed: (1) The Standing Committee proposed a motion to approve the letter from the Preparatory Committee for the Statue of General Architect of All Circles, seeking a public resolution from the Federation to dispatch a fundraising amount of 500 yuan and attach four donation registers, asking how the Federation should handle the matter. Resolved: Lu Jingshi, Zhang Yaoming, Ge Hecai, and Xu Shaochuan were appointed as four committee members responsible for fundraising. (2) Ge Hecai and Zhou Zixiang proposed to request the Municipal Department to forward to the Central Government that the holidays stipulated in the original labor contracts should remain valid in addition to the holidays promulgated by the National Government to avoid disputes. Resolved: Approved. (3) Ge Hecai and Zhou Zixiang proposed that a labor dispute occurred at the Samsung Cotton and Iron Factory, where the Fifth District Public Security Bureau dispatched a large number of police officers, interfered arbitrarily, used force to oppress workers, and arrested more than ten workers. This matter concerns the future of the labor movement and should be submitted to the Municipal Executive Committee to warn the Fifth District Public Security Bureau and inform the Public Security Bureau that such incidents should not occur again in the future to comply with democracy and protect the labor movement. Is this appropriate? Resolved: Approved. (4) The Standing Committee proposed to approve a letter from the Municipal Health Bureau requesting the dispatch of personnel to various factories to administer meningitis vaccinations, requesting the provision of two cars and the dispatch of three staff members to administer the injections separately, and asking how the car expenses should be paid. Resolved: Regarding car expenses, it was requested that the Municipal Executive Committee allocate funds separately. (5) Lu Jingshi and Zhou Zixiang proposed that twenty-three worker representatives from the Changxing Tobacco Factory came to the meeting to petition because the employer had closed the factory without reason, and they had not received any living expenses or retirement funds since the first day of the first lunar month, and their lives were in dire straits, requesting assistance. How should this be handled? Resolved: It was requested that the Municipal People's Training Association quickly forward the matter to the Municipal Government to convene both parties for arbitration. (6) Ge Hecai and Gu Yongquan proposed a case regarding the French imperialist police shooting and killing a worker at the Xiangchang Cotton Weaving Factory, asking how the Federation should express its stance. Resolved: A declaration should be issued. (7) Jin Yongchang proposed that the Municipal Party Department ordered the Federation to handle the Xiangchang Cotton Weaving Factory dispute. The Federation has dispatched personnel to convene both labor and management, and except for the issue of compensation for injuries, the rest has been completely resolved. Regarding the unresolved issue, how should the Federation handle it? Resolved: The resolution process should be reported to the higher authorities in writing. The issues of compensation for injuries should be handled by the Party and government organs in accordance with the orders of the Municipal Department. (8) The Standing Committee proposed a case based on a petition from the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union regarding the issue of unemployment placement in the industry, requesting assistance. It was found that the pharmaceutical employers were incorrigibly evil, and the Federation should make a serious statement to assist the workers. Resolved: It was requested that the Municipal Party Department severely punish the employers in the industry, dispatch personnel to provide assistance, and issue a circular to all trade unions to provide united assistance.

Grain Dealers Request Foreign Firms to Fulfill Orders

The foreign rice traded by various rice businesses in Shanghai is purchased from foreign firms. When the transaction is made, both parties sign an order stating the price and quantity of the goods. However, with the recent soaring rice prices, when merchants order foreign rice from foreign firms for future delivery, the firms often use the excuse that the goods have not arrived, causing disputes in the market from time to time. They had no choice but to report to the Chinese Grain Merchants Association, requesting strict enforcement. Yesterday, the association sent a letter to the foreign firms, stating: "To whom it may concern, our colleagues have ordered various amounts of foreign rice from your firms for different periods. According to usual practice, both parties issue orders specifying all procedures. However, these procedures are sometimes not strictly followed, leading to disputes between buyers and sellers from time to time. For the sake of seriousness, our association hereby sends you a special letter requesting that after the goods are loaded onto ships from their origin, you promptly notify the buying firms in writing of the name of the ship and the date of arrival in Shanghai, as usual, to facilitate business. We would be most grateful."

County Government Proclamation on Dredging Four Rivers

Zhang Da Jing, Zhu Jia Bang, Heng Gou River, and West Heng Jing

The Shanghai County Government recently received reports from Yang Jinghai, the head of the sixth district, stating that Shen Hanqing, the head of Yongjian Township, and Shen Xinguo, the deputy head of Yongjian Township; Yang Zhengxiang, the head of Xinhe Township, and Gu Sihe, the deputy head of Xinhe Township; Shen Haiqing, the head of Qingdeng Township, and Shen Danchun, the head of Wangtong Township, etc., had requested the dredging of four rivers: Zhang Da Jing, Zhu Jia Bang, Heng Gou River, and West Heng Jing. They requested that the matter be reviewed and filed, and a proclamation be issued to protect the project, and that funds be allocated for water draining and dam construction. It was found that the rivers proposed to be dredged by the township heads were indeed essential for farmland irrigation. Because they had not been dredged for many years, they were already silted up and impassable. Farmland needed water, but irrigation was impossible, and years of poor harvests were all due to this. Now, the township heads and their deputies have voluntarily initiated the dredging, showing enthusiasm for public welfare, which is commendable. Therefore, the original reports from the township heads and their deputies are copied and submitted to the county government for approval and filing, and a proclamation is issued to protect the project and allocate funds for water draining and dam construction to facilitate the project. County Magistrate Leng, after receiving the report, stated that since the rivers were indeed severely silted up, dredging them was an important water conservancy project. In addition to instructing the district head to approve the filing, he also issued a proclamation yesterday to inform all residents of the townships.

Fire on Tangshan Road Yesterday

A fire broke out at 10:50 AM yesterday at the residence of Huang Guangci in a bungalow at the intersection of Tangshan Road and Zhoushan Road in Hongkou, caused by a cigarette butt. At the time, the smoke was thick and the fire was intense. Fortunately, the Yangshupu Fire Brigade was nearby and rushed to the scene to put out the fire quickly.

Further Details on the Xietu Road Murder Case

Confirmed as Death Due to Cold Exposure While Intoxicated

A male corpse was found lying under a bamboo fence west of Mingde School on Xietu Road in Shanghai West. An official from the court was sent to investigate and determined that the death was due to cold exposure while intoxicated. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The details are now clarified and recorded below:

Background of the Deceased: The deceased was named Qiao Shitang, 22 years old, worked as a coppersmith, earned a monthly salary of 18 yuan, and was not yet married. He lived at No. 1 Qiaojiatang, West Xietu Road. His father, Qiao Zhenyu, was 57 years old and worked at the Wuzhou Solid Foundation Factory. His mother, Mrs. Zhu, had two sons and two daughters. The eldest son (the deceased), the second son was named Fuxiang, 17 years old. The eldest daughter married into the Lu family, and the second daughter, A Cui, was 26 years old and unmarried, working as a female worker at the Xi Heji Printing Factory on Tangjie. The family had newly built three bungalows and the family of five was relatively well-fed.

Drinking Together: On the evening of the 11th, at 8 PM, the deceased, along with friends Shen A Xiao, from No. 4 Gujia and the mountain store Su Xinyi from the Tongmao Vegetable shop in Ansi, (a Zhenjiang native from Xiaoyou Li) and the waiter A Di from Yile Tian Tea shop in Xujiahui, drank alcohol next to the tiger stove downstairs in the teahouse until 9:30 PM, when they dispersed. Shen A Xiao saw that Shitang was drunk and helped him to go home. At that time, there was a drizzle and it was difficult to see the direction. Passing by the Wudi Tou security team in Tushan Bay, they rested for a while and then continued to walk. Before they had gone far, Shitang stubbornly refused to go, shouting that he was hot and talking nonsense, appearing mad. He took off his black, straight-woven silk coat and trousers and lay on the ground. A Xiao tried to stop him, but he wouldn't listen. At that time, it was raining heavily, so he had no choice but to take the clothes and hats to the Qiao family, hoping to call his father to fetch him back. But when he arrived at the Qiao family, everyone was fast asleep. Zhenyu vaguely heard A Xiao's voice, saying that Shitang was drunk and should be fetched back quickly, but because the wind and rain were heavy, he did not go to check. A Xiao waited outside the door for a long time without any sound, so he went home to bed, in order to be at the shop at 4 AM the next morning.

Midnight Cries: After Shitang passed out, he woke up around 1 AM, but the cold had penetrated his bones, and he could not support himself, repeatedly shouting "Help, help!" Liu Genbao, a Jiangyin native living at No. 1, who was engaged in wood carving, was awakened from his dream and got up to open the door. He was shocked when he saw him, so he took Shitang's coat and put it on his lower body and helped him to the nearby security team. It was already closed. He transferred him to the home of Captain Ding, but Ding was also not there. Asked if he had any acquaintances, the deceased vaguely said that there were relatives working at the Yongxing Li Printing Factory. He was taken to the factory and then returned. The deceased then repeatedly called "Little sister, A Bao, help, help!" At that time, everyone was asleep, only the second landlord, Hua Xu, heard about it, but he did not dare to go out to look. Later, he went downstairs and left. At that time, two passersby, A and B, saw that the deceased's face was pale, so they left him at the corner of the wall. At this time, the deceased's sister, A Cui, and her friend Tao Xiubao, were returning home from work at the Xi Heji Printing Factory on Tangjie. Passing by the spot, they vaguely recognized her younger brother, but in the dark and because he was naked, they could not see clearly and hurried past, covering their faces.

Died After Falling to the Ground: At this time, the deceased was exhausted, and the cold rain poured down. His condition was critical, but he was still able to barely support himself, crawling to the bamboo fence of the Mingde School on Xietu Road, collapsing and dying.

Two Daughters Bringing Clothes: On the morning of the 12th, Zhang Xiaomei and Shen A Bao (cousins of the deceased), female workers at the Linxing Printing Factory, went to work at the factory. The second landlord, Hua Xu, told them about the events of the previous night and a fake straight-woven silk jacket (with a shoehorn and a towel inside) was picked up by the ladder. Recognizing the item, they knew it belonged to Shen A Xiao, but they should not call people in the middle of the night to reason with him. And take away the clothes. A Xiao was not there, so his brother Shen Linsheng said, "This coat belongs to Qiao Shitang." So he was sent to the Qiao family, handed over to the dead mother and returned. Mrs. Zhu saw that her son had not returned all night, went to A Xiao's house to look for him, did not find him, went to the police station to inquire, and only then did she know that he had died tragically.

Discovery of the Body: At 7 AM on the morning of the 12th, patrol chief Liu Kerang of the local police station led a police patrol to the bamboo fence west of Mingde School and found a male corpse lying on the ground. The sixth district, second branch was notified. Soon after, the corpse's mother arrived at the bureau for questioning: "Was there anyone drunk last night?" Mingde School, which issued the warning, had a male corpse. Mrs. Zhu went to identify it and confirmed that it was her son, and then burst into tears. Later, the local guarantor, Cao Zhongqing, reported the death to the court for examination.

A Glimpse of the Scene: The weather was fine on that day, and over two thousand people came to watch the scene. At 3 PM in the afternoon, Prosecutor Liu from the court and others went to the countryside to examine the body. It was determined that the death was due to suffocation from cold. He instructed the family to prepare a coffin for burial and then re-verify the death.

Tai Chi Expert Chen Ziming Arrives in Shanghai

There are two major schools of Tai Chi Chuan in Shanghai: one is the Yang Luchan school, now represented by Yang Chengfu, and the other is the Wu Yuxiang school, now represented by Sun Lutang. Luchan learned from Chen Changxing of Chenjiagou, Wen County, Henan. Now, Chen Ziming, also from Chenjiagou, is a descendant of Chen Bu, a figure from the early Ming Dynasty who mastered Tai Chi Chuan. The Chen family has produced many famous individuals over the generations and benefited from Chen Changxing's cultivation. Chen Ziming is particularly accomplished. Chen Ziming, in his prime, visited famous teachers all over China, covering half the country. As a result, his skills are even more refined. Because the Chinese people admire martial arts, and Shanghai is a thriving center for promotion, Chen Ziming is willing to dedicate his skills and teach publicly wherever he goes. Chen is currently residing at the residence of Mr. Jiang Zicheng at Lao Ziji Lu, Mengdelan Road. Those who wish to learn can contact Mr. Jiang.

Various Organizations Initiate Memorial for Madam Zhong Ketuo

Madam Tu Huizhen, wife of Zhong Ketuo, a member of the Central Opium Prohibition Committee, passed away in November of last year. The Central Opium Prohibition Committee, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, the National Christian Council of China, the Qingxin Girls' School Alumni Association, St. Peter's Church in Shanghai, St. Paul's Church in Nanjing, and other six organizations have jointly initiated a memorial service for Madam Tu Huizhen, wife of Zhong Ketuo. Notices have been distributed, and the memorial service is scheduled to be held at 3 PM on the 16th of this month (Sunday) at St. Peter's Church, No. 11 Avenyue Road. The preparatory office is located at Room 112, No. 4 Hong Kong Road, Shanghai.

Minutes of the Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Chinese Medicine Association

The Shanghai Special Municipal Chinese Medicine Association held its fourth joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees on the 13th of this month. The meeting began at 8 PM. Xu Xiangren and Gu Weichuan were elected as chairmen. The meeting proceeded as usual. Items reported: (omitted) Proposed discussions: A. Regarding the March 17 Memorial Meeting, in addition to the five standing committee members and the chairman of the Supervisory Committee who will be responsible for preparing for and attending the conference, should additional representatives be sent? Resolved: Six additional representatives will be sent. Zhu Weiju, Chen Shuan, Chen Cunren, Zhang Deyi, Wang Meisheng, and Gong Hanwen were immediately nominated as the six representatives. B. Labor-management disputes in the pharmaceutical industry have re-emerged, causing strikes, indirectly affecting the medical community and hindering patients. How should the Association express its position? Resolved: A request will be submitted to the Municipal Government to quickly stop the pharmaceutical industry unrest in order to protect the social patients. C. How should the memorial cards and slogans forwarded by the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association for the March 17 Memorial be distributed? Resolved: The memorial cards will be distributed by the executive and supervisory committee members of the Association, with a charge of one yuan per hundred cards. The slogans will be distributed by the Shenzhou, Zhonghua, and Chinese Medicine Associations to their members for posting. D. Xia Chongguang proposed: (1) Should charitable organizations that provide medical services hire members of the Association to serve as medical staff? Resolved: To be transferred to the Standing Committee for discussion. (2) Should the Association establish a medical research institute to enhance the knowledge of its members? Resolved: A letter will be sent to the Shenzhou, Zhonghua, and Chinese Medicine Associations to establish their own institutes separately. (3) Should the Association request the Health Bureau to ban shamans and witches, protect the lives of the people, and protect the professions of medical practitioners and doctors? Resolved: A request will be submitted to the Health Bureau to ban them in accordance with the regulations. E. Should the Association appoint additional personnel to edit the annual publication? Resolved: It will be jointly edited by the Secretarial Department and the Finance Department. This case will be submitted to the Standing Committee for reconsideration. The meeting adjourned at 10 PM.

New Equipment for the Labor Hospital

The Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road in Shanghai West, in addition to purchasing ultraviolet light and artificial sun lamps for the chemotherapy department and recently ordering X-ray equipment, has also purchased a patient transport vehicle from Yichang Automobile Company for approximately 4,000 yuan to facilitate patient transportation. The vehicle has already been delivered to the hospital and will be put into service upon receipt of the notification from the Municipal Government.

Japanese Child Killed by Car

At noon the other day, a car numbered 6542 was speeding along Gordon Road when it knocked down a Japanese girl, crushing her vital organs, and she died instantly. The police investigation revealed that the driver, Cheng A Tao from Tongzhou, was arrested and taken to the Gordon Road police station. Yesterday morning, the car driver was sent to the Provisional Court. After a brief interrogation by Judge Luo, the defendant was ordered to be detained pending a joint trial with the Japanese consulate. It is learned that the deceased was named Shi Qiangmaila, only eight years old. Yesterday, the Japanese Consulate sent personnel to the mortuary to verify the body, notified the family, and ordered them to claim the body for burial.

Li Rongsheng Acquitted and Released

Hua Gensheng from Suzhou and Li Rongsheng from Zhenjiang were arrested by detectives from the Hongkou police station at the Fairy World amusement park and charged with leading gangs to rob the residents of No. 182 Fuzhou Road, No. 52 Shanhai Pass Road, and No. 1729 North Chengdu Road. The Provisional Court repeatedly brought them in for trial. Lawyer Li Yanzhan Ji Feng defended Li, saying that Li had been a chef in the vegetable section of the amusement park and had not engaged in any theft. The verdict was reserved for a later date. Yesterday morning, Lawyer Zhan went to the Fifth Court to await the verdict. Judge Tan then took the bench and ordered Hua and Li to be brought forward. Hua Ronggen was found guilty of three counts of robbery, each punishable by seven years of imprisonment, to be served concurrently for a total of nine years, and was deprived of his civil rights for nine years. Li Rongsheng was acquitted and released.

Gang of Thieves Detained for Further Investigation

A gang of thieves was hiding in the Pingjiang Hotel on Hubei Road, and was arrested by the Lao Zha Police Station the other day. Yesterday morning, the thieves Sun Mingyue, Zhang Yingzhou, Rong Arong, Yang Zhenkang, Li Yutang, Mei Renshu, Xie Rusong, Wang Ziyou, Bian Zijun, Dong Songlang, Shi Jinfa, Yu Ruihao, and twelve others, along with two real and fake pistols and seven bullets, were taken to the Provisional Court. After a brief interrogation by Judge Gao Junxiang, they were ordered to be detained for further investigation for fourteen days. Shi Jinfa was arrested at No. 1338 Xiude Lane in the French Concession after Sun and the other ten were arrested. Yu Ruihao was arrested last at Room 30 of the First Hotel on Zhejiang Road. The pistols and bullets were also found in that room.

Slapping a Woman's Cheek Costs 35 Yuan

The Wang Jinmei Insult Case

Wang Jinmei, the director of female receptionists at the Little World, was beaten by the rogue Zhang Genbao and his gang near the Great Bell in the French Concession on the 9th of this month. The police arrested Zhang and took him to the police station. Yesterday, he was sent to the French Court for prosecution. The plaintiff, Wang Jinmei, stated that on that day, she was on her way home from Little World when she was suddenly slapped on the cheek from behind by Zhang Genbao, whom she did not know, at the intersection of Madian Road near the Great Bell. She immediately shouted loudly, and the police arrived and caught him. At that time, her watch was also lost. She requested an investigation. The defendant's lawyer argued on his behalf that the plaintiff was working as a female receptionist at Little World. The defendant and several friends went to play there and had a conflict due to teasing, which led to a quarrel. At that time, the plaintiff called the police and brutally beat the defendant and others, causing injuries. Therefore, he was angry and waited for her in the controlled area and beat the plaintiff to vent his anger. It was purely revenge and there was no robbery of her watch. The defendant was young and ignorant, and requested leniency. The defendant Zhang Genbao testified that his friends told him to beat her, and the rest of his testimony was evasive. The plaintiff, Yu Jinmei, also stated that she was not a receptionist, but the director, and had never had any teasing or quarrels with anyone. The defendant's lawyer's statements were false, and requested investigation. Presiding Judge Zhu sentenced the defendant Zhang Genbao to a fine of 35 yuan.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky was mostly cloudy, and there might be thunder in the Yangtze River Basin. The sky south of Ma'an Island was overcast and the wind was nondirectional, with occasional fog. The westerly wind along the coast of Shandong and here was quite strong. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 66.2 degrees, and the lowest was 44.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 56.4 degrees, and the lowest was 23.5 degrees.

Letter

To the Editor,

Having read in your newspaper's local news column a report that detectives from the French Concession police arrested bandits on the upper floor of the Dahua Middle School, we have found that the building leased by our school is in the rear and has nothing to do with where the bandits lived. We are sincerely afraid of being misled by rumors, which would affect the reputation of our school. Therefore, we are writing specifically to correct this. We hope you will publish this for us.

The fourteenth day.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Seafarer

Master: I rang the bell for quite a while. Why are you always so slow to come?

Servant: Master, I just fell down the stairs.

Master: In that case, you saved some steps. You should have come even faster. Why are you late instead?

Guest: Who is in charge of your company?

Waiter: Who is in charge? I don't know. I am often the one being blamed.

Door-to-door peddler: Sir/Madam, look at how good this batch of goods is. Would you like me to deliver more to you?

Housewife: Come back next Friday to discuss it.

Peddler: Sorry, I happen to be going to Suzhou that day.

Housewife: Because I happen not to be home that day either.

Train Passenger A: Sir, are you going to sit here all the way?

Train Passenger B: I paid for my ticket. I sit where I find a seat. How can you interfere with me?

Train Passenger A: But you are sitting on my hat.

Father: Child, let me ask you. When you are sitting on the tram and you see an old lady come up, what do you do?

Child: I close my eyes and pretend to be asleep.

Glimpses of the Capital

— Wei

Since the suspension of bus services in the capital, there has been no news of their resumption for several months. It is presumably due to poor business and excessive embezzlement. However, the distance from Xiaguan to the city is more than ten miles. Although there are small trains, carriages, cars, and rickshaws, people in the middle class are generally unwilling to use them, as they are not as cheap and fast as buses. Therefore, since the suspension, the general public has suffered, and the carriage and rickshaw businesses have undoubtedly doubled their profits. However, those who are familiar with the roads and experienced in traveling around the capital still take cars, and the fares are equivalent to those of buses. However, these cars are not "public" but "wild chicken" cars.

Over the past year, the film industry has sprung up like bamboo shoots after rain, with names like National, World, Nanjing, New Light, Datong, and Central. The best performer is National, due to its superior location and seating. World, Datong, and Nanjing also show many famous films. However, the previous screenings of "King of Kings," "The Ten Commandments," and "Ben-Hur" generated considerable profit but later caused great resentment. The authorities subsequently issued a ban on "King of Kings." Recently, a film censorship bureau has also been established.

The roads in the capital, except for Zhongshan Avenue, are generally not good. Since the beginning of spring, continuous rain has made them muddy and difficult to travel, especially when cars pass, splashing black mud everywhere. Even if one avoids them by more than ten feet, one can still get covered in mud. When meeting on a narrow road, one can only sigh helplessly. Due to the heavy traffic and excessive loads, there is occasional erosion on Zhongshan Road as well.

Although the cost of living in the capital is increasing daily, the price of food is still relatively cheap. However, due to the rain this spring, prices have gradually risen. The current price of ordinary rice is around fifteen yuan per picul, leading to increased food costs in various institutions or unsatisfactory and unappetizing meals. The common people are crying out in hardship.

The most famous hotels in the city have always been the Anle Hotel and others. Recently, since the opening of the Central Hotel, the scale has become even grander. The high-powered electric lights shining at night can be seen from afar, adding to the commercial splendor of the capital. The World Hotel is also under construction near Menlian Bridge near Hua Pai Lou, and there will surely be a more intense competition in the future.

A Record of Plum Blossom Viewing in Dingli

— Listening to Eternal Life

People only know that the plum blossoms in Hangzhou must be counted as those on Gushan and Lingfeng, but they do not know that Chao Mountain, west of Linping, is even more worthy of seeing. Even if they know about the plum blossoms on Chao Mountain, they must count the Song plum tree in the Great Hall of Bao'en Temple as unique. But they do not know that south of Ma'an Mountain, there is a village called Dingli, which has even more to offer. This spring, Monk Shipiao sent a letter inviting me to visit Chao Mountain, saying that the thirty miles of jade flowers were as bright as snow, and the fragrant breeze moved, clearing the lungs and heart. This was not something to be missed. Thus, my heart was stirred, and I invited Deng Fenweng, Wang Lunfu, and Tang Xian to go together. For seven hours, the train transported us from Shanghai, and we spent the night at the Da Yuan Temple. The next morning, there was a heavy fog. All the mountains were asleep. In the hazy and indistinct light, the sun came out with halo clouds, and wild birds chirped from time to time. We walked together in the mountain belly amidst the diffuse fog. The distant fragrance had already arrived with the east wind. The follower carried a jar of wine and five sets of utensils. The snacks were selected from turtle doves, wild ducks, beef jerky, peanuts, and the like. We drank along the way. Soon, thousands and thousands of trees were hung with copper bells. The mountain mist gradually cleared, and shadows of people were everywhere. The faint smoke and slender jade, quietly wafting cold fragrance, also gradually came into view. Moreover, between Qian Bieyun, short fences, and sparse bamboo fences, one or two branches stretched obliquely across the road, blocking my hat brim. So I also lowered my head to pass. Reading the public's line "People are still unyielding towards daffodils, how dare they not bow their heads when they see you," I was moved by it. After walking about a mile, we drank by the White Horse Pit, laying a cup of wine under the plum tree. Arriving in Dingli, the branches and twigs were disordered all the way, and the profuse blossoms were horizontal and vertical. The flowing light at the bottom of my eyes was not inferior to the salt flakes. Arriving at this village of cold fragrance and solitary beauty, I doubted whether I was not stranded in a rugged and desolate place. Its power to shift emotions and relieve suffering was greater than drinking ten thousand bells of wine. The sun gradually rose, and we sat down in a harmonious position. We agreed not to walk, took futons, and sat cross-legged in the midst of ten thousand flowers. The sound of bees was there or not. The forest breeze entered the wine. We held our breath and tasted it quietly, unaware of the evening.

Overseas Plum Blossom News

— Lai

Mei Lanfang, the king of the Chinese opera world, and his party of twenty-one people arrived in New York on February 9 to perform in the United States. Wu Chaoshu, our minister to the United States, believed that Mei Jun's trip carried the important mission of promoting Chinese art and bridging Eastern and Western cultures. He hosted a banquet at the embassy on the evening of February 14 to welcome them. That evening at 10:00, a grand reception was held at a famous hotel in Washington, inviting Mei Jun to perform. American dignitaries, senators, and ambassadors and ministers from diplomatic missions were invited in advance to watch the performance, so that Westerners could gain a deep understanding of Eastern art. Except for President Hoover and his wife, who were out fishing and had not returned, the invitees included Vice President Curtis and his sister, Mrs. Gann, the wife of former President Wilson, the Secretary of the Interior and his wife, the Secretary of Commerce and his wife, the Acting Secretary of the Navy and his wife, the French Ambassador and his wife, the German Ambassador and his wife, the Italian Ambassador and his wife, the Japanese Ambassador and his wife, the Turkish Ambassador, the Cuban Ambassador and his wife, the Spanish Ambassador and his wife, the Chilean Ambassador and his wife, and the Swiss, Finnish, Panamanian, Egyptian, Bulgarian, Venezuelan, Albanian, Dominican, Polish, Dutch, Norwegian, Siamese, Paraguayan, Ecuadorian, Nicaraguan, South African Republic, and other countries' ministers and their wives, the Undersecretary of State and the undersecretaries of various departments and their wives, many senators, the chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, Mr. Potter, and many representatives, as well as five hundred people, including naval and army officers and social celebrities. The splendor of the occasion was unprecedented. The performances of "Chang'e Flying to the Moon" and "A Thousand Pieces of Gold for a Smile" were greeted with thunderous applause. It was considered something never seen before. This was the first meeting between Mei Jun's art and the American people. Mei Jun then returned to New York by car at one o'clock that night and was scheduled to perform there on the seventeenth.

The Second Day of the Bee Painting Exhibition

— Swallow

The Bee Painting Society's exhibition opened on the Flower Day.

Fine rain and slanting wind, few guests. Until the second day, the sky cleared and the rain stopped. In the afternoon, those who bought tickets to enter the venue came one after another, exceptionally crowded. Before four o'clock, more than two hundred tickets had been sold, which can be described as a great success. The paintings displayed at the venue were even more exquisite than on the first day. Among the works of the society members, Qian Shoutie's Huangshan landscape folding screen was the most magnificent. The viewers were crowded around it. Sun Xueni's landscape followed the style of Xiang Huaishu Mei. The large painting displayed this time was entirely in the style of Shitao. The brushwork was bold and thick, which was completely different from the past. It was indeed a masterpiece. Zheng Wuchang and Xu Weibai transformed brush and ink into smoke and clouds, with the beauty of different tunes played with equal skill. In particular, Zheng's painting of silkworms and mulberry and Xu's painting of red plum blossoms were more transcendent with less strokes. Jiang Runsheng's Orphan Picture was vividly lifelike and could be considered a masterpiece. Qiu Zhixiang's imitation of Shitao's landscape, painted on Goryeo paper, showed even more skill. The best of the figure paintings were Hu Sanqiao's "Adding Incense" and He Tianjian's "This Night, Listening to the Sounds at Xie's House." One imitated Yu Hu, and the other copied Xiaolou. Bai Longshanren also had three exquisite paintings on display, especially the chrysanthemums and sparrows. Zhang Shanzi and Zhang Daqian's brothers were exquisite in painting tigers, horses, landscapes, and flowers. This was most rare. Others such as Ma Wanli's flowers and Ye Weixin's landscapes were all outstanding young artists. As for the ancient paintings, there were even more and more exquisite than on the first day. Bada Shanren and Shitao Liangfeng were the most numerous. Others such as Huishu, Cangshuo, Tiesheng, Baiyang, Nansha, Ruobo, Shuwen, Zhuxu, and Dongxin, each painting was a treasure and a wonderful work. It was like entering a mountain of treasures. It was a pity that it was too late and I could not see them all. I will briefly record what I saw.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (7)

— Linghua

On the morning of the fifteenth, I visited Liang Zhongheng of the Overseas Chinese Daily. Mr. Liang was enthusiastic and patriotic, and his words were sad. The people of Yunnan still have protectors because they have a master to rely on. What can we Chinese rely on? You are traveling on the road. If someone attacks, where can you seek protection? The Chinese revolution has been going on for many years. Overseas Chinese have donated millions of dollars. Up to now, they have not been able to negotiate with the French to set up a consulate. Diplomacy has failed so much. Internal strife is the daily routine, and overseas Chinese are allowed to be slaves without question. Alas! I was saddened by his words. In the afternoon, I visited Mr. Qun, who said that the manuscript must be submitted to the police station for inspection before 2:00 PM before it can be published. Therefore, I was unable to see it. In short, the press is very dissatisfied with the endless Chinese civil war.

Mr. Chen of Qun Bao talked about the situation of the overseas Chinese, saying that there were a total of 300,000 people in Annam, 20,000 in Saigon, and 100,000 in Dikean. Dikean is Chinatown. The overseas Chinese property is mainly rice exports. It is called rice, but the capital is often millions of dollars. It is sold to ports in the Pacific Ocean. Shanghai and Guangdong also eat their rice. The so-called Annam rice is divided into five groups: the Guangzhao Group, the Chaozhou Group, the Fujian Group, and the Hakka Group. The number of Cantonese is seven, and the number of Fujianese is three, but the wealth of Fujianese is better. The autonomous groups are the General Chamber of Commerce and schools, about five or six, such as the Decheng Middle School and the French School, which are middle school level. However, others say that there are considerable restrictions on higher education here, which means that it is not easy to run a school, or perhaps the level of education here does not have high-level knowledge. According to the female principal, there are three or four girls' schools in total, but old-style private schools are everywhere, just like the use of the lunar calendar.

On the sixteenth, a Sunday, Huang Qiting, the supervisory committee member of the Annam Kuomintang General Branch, and Feng Mingfen, the principal of the Yonglong Provincial School, came to talk to me at the Zhenhua Girls' School. They mentioned my theory of the World Kunhua Datong Federation, and that the press should publicly disseminate it, which is related to the gospel of human peace. Even the French government has no objection. I said that I have already printed a French translation of the outline, but it was sent to Singapore. The translation was proofread and printed by Shen Zhongjun, an old French expert in Shanghai. The French consul in Shanghai saw it and was greatly surprised, saying that we in the West have made many inventions, but we have not thought of a way to avoid war. Let you Orientals invent it. I still want the original book to be translated into French. I also talked to the manager of the French Daily in Shanghai for a while, and he also said that he was very happy to get this news. The French love freedom, and if there is a good method, they will welcome it. Today's world is killing each other, and it is also because there is no good way to escape. It is not that people have hatred for each other. The method should be discussed by the public.

A Poem of Seventy Rhymes on Angola

— Cheng Yansheng wrote in New Capital, Turkey (December, Year 18)

Vast is Turkey, geographically blocking East and West.

Seven hundred years since its founding, thirty-six generations have passed. (Turkey was founded by the Ottoman Emperor and passed down for 36 generations until its demise in 1922.)

The wind and clouds converged in a great upheaval, and the prestige led the clans.

Emperor Osman, with his heroic plans, was blessed.

The imperial family suddenly declined, and the criminal administration lost its balance.

The unbuilt was eventually ruined, becoming prey for the strong.

The unprecedented European War began, and the national power was increasingly oppressed.

Its territories were all divided, and the boundaries were arbitrarily clipped.

Greece showed its old resentment, and its dazzling soldiers came even closer.

The British followed behind, and the crisis was truly unpredictable. (The Greek-Turkish War began in 1919, and the British actually dominated it.)

The hearts of the people had not completely died, and the three households of Qin could be restored.

Heroes rose up and restored the old business in one battle. (The current Turkish President Kemal raised troops in eastern Asia Minor, and finally defeated the Western Greek army near Angola. After the great victory, the enemy was broken, and the remaining bandits all fled.)

Seated in the ancient capital (In 1920, the Angola government was established, and Kemal was the speaker of the National Assembly), directing the heart and belly.

At that time, trust was difficult, and the wounds were lamented and filled with eyes.

The tragic Luo Qunying, relying on bamboo to form warp and weft.

A few days to revive the old brigade, a few days to inspect the people and shepherds.

A few days to praise the state, a few days to drive out the clan.

Announcing the republic and expelling the Sultan religious leader, he is truly a powerful person, who can turn the valleys by hand.

Suddenly the whole situation was settled, and the sky was solemn.

Internal networks have been managed, but diplomacy is not easy to resolve.

The great powers met in Lausanne (The Lausanne Conference was held in Europe in 1922 to resolve the Eastern Question), relying on frustration.

Zheng Qiao was selected as an envoy, and Cao Zhitan was listed (The Turkish representative was General Ismet, the current Prime Minister.)

National rights cannot be lost, and national shame must eventually be avenged.

Jin and Chu still think of invading, and the covenant has been torn several times (The conference did not allow the demands of the Turkish representatives. Negotiations were interrupted and resumed the following year. The treaties were concluded equally.)

Weeping and recovering the old capital, the national spirit has since been alive (In October 1923, Turkish troops re-entered Constantinople, and the people welcomed them with tears).

Striving to join the great powers, reform and advance the martyrs.

A distant guest came from thousands of miles away, relying on light chariots to hear and see.

The future bears good fortune, and the sightseeing is gratifying.

The luggage is worth the cold winter, and the trudging is not tiring.

Setting off in the morning at the Hei Sea, arriving in the evening at the Zhuangji County (Angola).

Lodging in the secluded building in the hostel, driving to the Guangdian.

Suddenly the city is prosperous, controlling the border and the dangerous.

The expression is stubbornly locked, and the passes are moving like lightning.

The shape is superior to West Asia, and the collar connects three continents (Angola is surrounded by mountains and its shape is dangerous, which can control the key points of the three continents of Europe, Africa, and Asia).

Determining hegemony, the heart struggles, and the power to invite success can be aided. (The Greeks, Persians, Romans, Seljuks, and Arabs have all occupied this land.)

Seeing the ancient battlefield, the ramparts turned empty.

The suburban drinking water cave, always watching the water filling the pond.

The old vines rise to the pine forest, and the hawks and falcons soar in the clouds. (History records that the Roman master Pang and the Anxi King Miderdati, the Mongolian Timur and the Turkish Sultan Baya Jide all used troops here.)

Seeing the ancient imperial palace, the Chongji Yinling is occupied.

Other generations mourn loneliness, imagining the image. (History records that King Alexander of Macedon once held meetings with monarchs and ministers of various countries twice in this capital. The old site of the palace on the rock still exists.)

Huabiao met for thousands of years, and the ruined walls survived the ruins. (The column of the Roman Emperor Augustus and his living temple are still there.)

Engraving the King's Meeting Picture, the cold sun shines on the stone slabs. (A large number of ancient steles are piled up on the side of the temple, all depicting the stories of the Greek, Roman, Persian, and other world dynasties, hunting and riding. Unfortunately, they cannot be rubbed.)

The ancients are gone, and the new state is established today.

The cultural relics follow the Thai West, and the clothes of the dynasty and the field change (reforming the text and abolishing the red crown).

The track is strategic for transportation, and the well market is vigorously repaired.

What are the three things? The six prefectures are especially lush. (Angola is building municipal facilities in the new district. Everything is available for residents, such as electric lights, gas, and running water. The Presidential Palace, State Council, Parliament, and various departments are newly built and heavily planted with trees.)

The garden is full of frost flowers (although the park has entered winter, there are still autumn flowers).

The itchy order is full of lectures, and the bronze statue casts a great medal. (There is a bronze statue of General Kemal at the entrance of the new city, which is heroic.)

The official road is as flat as a grindstone, and the Hua houses are scattered everywhere.

The ring is full of crystal salt, and the brocade felt is dazzling.

Fresh fruit pushes gold lemon, and plain silk unfolds beautiful silk (both are the products of the land).

He is happy to follow the rule of law, and public and private friends are happy.

It can be a great success in ten years, and prosperity is expected to be the same.

My thoughts are difficult to express, and my intentions are good.

I will not stay in Yu for a long time, and I will come to Yu for the rest of my life.

Looking back at the homeland, the love in my heart turns.

There have been twenty years of upheaval, and the north and south are still coated with charcoal.

How can we bear to wield the same chamber sword, and not solve the hanging problem.

Singing generously and weeping, when will the Yu domain feast?

Commonly known as two sick men, one sick man has been released.

Ming Xiaozou Dao Gui, who has been a good doctor. (Europeans call Turkey and China two sick men in East Asia)

Lying across the red county map, the colors of mountains and rivers are dim.

And I got General Kai. (Refers to Kemal) He resisted the thieves with his festival.

Lai Erji cares for danger, and Lai Erxing's country.

The Han and Tang dynasties have been buried, and the Song and Ming dynasties have been trapped in accumulated habits.

The masses have been in decline for a long time, and the husband should be responsible.

The Yellow Emperor is hanging in the sky, and the descendants may not be wrong.

Zhongshan is broad and magnificent.

Commercial News

Financial Spot Gold Slightly Declines

After the initial record, it was weak, and the situation of yesterday's spot gold was changing from strong to weak. There were advances and retreats from time to time. In the morning market, there were three and a half taels high and low, and in the afternoon market, there were also about three taels. The buying and selling among the industry was not enthusiastic, because in the forward trading season, Yongchenchang, Fuyu, Taixing, Dadecheng, etc. all had sales, and Yuanheng, Shunli, Chunyuan Yong, Yuanmaoyong, etc. were all buyers. As for foreign exchange, it changed from steady to flat and weak. Since the large volumes in the early market saw an increase, the silver price shrank instead, so the market opened high. After that, buyers were more frequent, and it once exceeded 498 taels. Later, the selling pressure was strong, and foreign exchange also turned into a large movement, so it fell sharply by more than three taels. In the afternoon market, it became increasingly weak, and the bills were weak, and the transaction was even more quiet. Hengxing, Shunlifengyong, etc. sold some, and Yanyu, Fuyu, and some small households bought a little, so the price suddenly retreated to within 9,004 taels, and finally pulled up about two taels.

At the beginning of the morning, because the US silver fell, it opened high. Yesterday, the London silver bars were not more recent, and the distant term had increased by one-eighth. The silver price was reduced by one-eighth, so the opening of the spot gold in April added one or two cents, which was 496 taels and six cents. Later, the internal slightly loosened, and Sumitomo bought forward Japanese gold at 1 tael, 0 points, 2 points and 5 points, so it dropped by 1 tael. After 1,000 points, it was 97 taels and two cents. After a while, it increased by eight or nine cents, which was 98 taels and one cent. After 10:30, the bills were especially loose, but it was not easy to sell them, and the people's hearts showed weakness because of this. It dropped by a total of three taels, and at 11:45, it was only 95 taels, two or three cents. The afternoon market was weak, and the closing fell by a small one tael. The afternoon market opened at 95 taels and eight cents, followed by an increase of five or six cents, which was 96 taels and four cents. Then, due to the sale of retail investors, it fell to 95 taels, four or five cents. Gold Exchange Ban on Off-Exchange Forward Transactions

This session's forward trading was changed to the day before (the 15th) because the 16th fell on a Sunday. Unexpectedly, certain firms had already privately engaged in forward trading yesterday, with bulls paying premiums estimated at around one tael or less. The exchange's board of directors discovered this and, considering that member firms should not conduct transactions privately before the designated date, immediately notified the brokers' association to stop the practice. A special announcement was also issued, stating, "According to Article 42 of Chapter 10 of the amended business regulations of this exchange, forward trading is to be rolled over to the next month's period on the 16th of each month, etc. Since the 16th of this month falls on a Sunday, the brokers' association was previously permitted to temporarily suspend operations on that day and reschedule the forward trading to the 15th. This has already been announced to the market. However, this morning, off-exchange forward trading occurred, which constitutes behavior that intentionally disrupts the market, as stipulated in Article 50, Item 1 of Chapter 12 (Penalty Provisions) of the business regulations. It is also equivalent to violating this exchange's articles of association, business regulations, other regulations and instructions, and the brokers' association's bylaws, as stated in Item 2. In addition to notifying the brokers' association to immediately hold an emergency meeting to strictly prohibit this practice and to investigate the broker(s) who initially disrupted market order today, further action will be taken. This announcement is hereby made."

By the afternoon close, compared to the previous day, both shillings and US dollars had leveled off, while Japanese yen slightly decreased by 0.125. However, the difference between March and June forward rates was more than half a percentage point. Chinese merchants' speculative trading was scarce because the forward trading date was approaching, and the May premium had already opened. The afternoon trading was particularly quiet. Furthermore, due to disturbances in the market related to premiums pre-opening for forward trading, buying and selling became even more stagnant.

Overnight Interest Rates Remain Unchanged

Market Overview: For several days, due to scarce transactions, the market has been sluggish, prices have been quiet, and the situation has been indecisive. At this time of the spring equinox, in past years, there would have been potential for development. However, this year, because the native banks once experienced difficulties, they are now mostly taking a wait-and-see approach, unwilling to rashly forge ahead. This has led to a quiet market, despite the potential for significant development, which is regrettable. However, bank settlements are comparable to last year, indicating that they are unrelated to the recent native bank crisis.

Overnight Interest Rates: The morning "foreign interest rate" was 72.0375 thousandths, and the annual rate was 2.5 thousandths, with only a 1.25 thousandth difference between the morning and afternoon rates. "Silver interest rates" for both morning and afternoon sessions for transferring silver were uniformly at 6 thousandths, a slight improvement of 1 thousandth compared to the previous day. Bank-listed rates showed no significant market activity, with only 2 to 3 thousandths of added premium.

Sales are somewhat stagnant. Although some merchant groups are interested, they are temporarily holding back due to the unfavorable market conditions. Business is slightly lacking. However, the Tianjin merchants are still actively purchasing.

The selling pressure in the standard yarn market is high. The market opened with a slight drop in American cotton and rumors about the current situation. Grain and Wheat Market, Futures and Spot Both Small

Yesterday, after the opening of the rice and wheat market in the morning and afternoon, prices were slightly sluggish in all months due to the smaller volume of imported wheat. However, sellers of near and far months did not flood the market. Bulls ultimately picked up cheap buys, and far months were considered distant. Although the weather was good, it was not enough to drive the market significantly. Therefore, the fluctuations were minimal. As in past years, the future new wheat market is likely to soften. As a result, the current month was down 0.02 compared to the previous day, April was down 0.01, July was down 0.01, and there were no other changes. Spot wheat trading was active, and prices were slightly lower. If the quality of the subsequent shipments is not good, prices may still need to increase somewhat. The opening prices were 5.16 taels per package for Suzhou wheat, 5.15 taels for Qingjiangpu wheat, 5.04 taels for Yangzhou wheat, 5.12 to 5.1 taels for Shaoxing wheat, 5.02 taels for Jiangxi wheat (lower quality down to 4.8 taels), and 5.12 to 5.045 taels for Gaoyou wheat. A total of 4,500 packages were offered, purchased by Fufeng and other factories.

Primary Cause of Stagnant Flour Market

Imported Wheat Prices Continue to Decline

Tianjin Merchants Liquidate Futures Positions

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, prices for all months trended toward stagnation again. This was due to the continued decline in imported wheat prices, which dampened market sentiment. As for sales in the north, the Yingkou merchants bought over 10,000 packages in the morning, so the current month showed some stability. However, in the afternoon, because the Tianjin merchants had already purchased spot goods, they slightly liquidated some futures positions. Therefore, prices for all months were slightly softer than in the morning. The prices for far months were also slightly softer due to the sunny weather. Looking at the future situation, because there is ultimately a surplus of imported wheat, the local flour market is likely to fluctuate within a range. As a result, the current month was down 0.0075 compared to the previous day, April was down 0.005, May was unchanged, June was up 0.0025, July was down 0.005, and August was down 0.005.

Imported Rice Rises by 0.2 Yuan

Futures Rice Up About 0.01 Yuan

Yesterday, the imported rice market saw another change. After three new ships arrived, merchants from Jiangbei and other inland areas actively purchased rice, and prices immediately jumped by 0.2 yuan. Futures rice saw limited supply and high demand, and prices rose in response. Traders from inland areas also paid attention to far-month rice, and both near-month and far-month prices rose by about 0.01 yuan per dan. The prices were 14 yuan to 13.93 yuan for 6,000 packages of No. 1 and No. 2 Saigon rice, 14.6 to 14.4 yuan for 4,000 packages of No. 1 rice. Jiafu rice was newly arrived, and due to the lack of high-quality, medium-quality, and low-quality rice, 5,000 packages were offered at 13.35 yuan. 10,000+ packages of futures Saigon rice were offered, with No. 1 road cargo at 14.28 yuan, No. 2 at 13.75 yuan, 30,000 packages of small-sized rice with road cargo at 13.63 yuan, and 6.08 to 6.05 yuan for March/April, 2,000 packages of large-sized road cargo at 12.95 yuan.

The imported rice market has been volatile lately. Prices tend not to weaken before road cargo arrives. Once new goods arrive, prices rise sharply. The reason for this surge is that various groups compete to purchase the goods once they arrive.

Northern Goods from Two Gates: Candied Dates Market in Decline

Candied dates sold for 26-27 taels in early spring, but have since declined. Recently, the decline has accelerated. As the weather warms, there is a risk that the quality of these sugared confections will deteriorate. In the current sluggish market, prices must decline. Yesterday, top-quality candied dates were selling for less than 20 taels, with slight increases for lower grades. The Lanxi goods were even weaker and seemed to be in irreversible decline.

Silk and Tea: Chinese Silk Continues to Be Exported

Previously, local European firms had temporarily halted silk exports due to the decline in the exchange rate of shillings, etc., and the low overseas silk prices. The export of Chinese silk was thus stagnant. Now that the exchange rate has strengthened and the Yokohama Japanese silk prices have risen, European and American silk prices have gradually trended upward. Furthermore, as British and American postal ships are successively exporting goods, exporters are dividing their existing silk inventory into batches for export. In addition to Anli and other firms shipping 250 pieces of Chinese silk on the British postal ship Alipore to British Bombay today, Ganli, Lan Lebi, and others will ship 600 pieces of yellow, white, and gray silk on the American postal ship Pias to Seattle tomorrow. This has also activated silk sales to Europe and America. Yesterday, there was a telegram reporting from Shanghai that Ganli and others were importing 60 packages of medium-grade Shanghai factory silk and 50 packages of gray silk, with strong prices.

Shanghai Market

Business News

Hanli Company's Latest Invention - Zhongling Imprinting Machine: Hanli Company, located at 216 Sichuan Road, claims that their newly invented domestic pneumatic Zhongling imprinting machine has been attracting a continuous stream of visitors, buyers, and out-of-town orders. The company is struggling to keep up with demand. As a result, Manager Gao has been working day and night to increase production. The number of shipments has increased several times compared to when the company first started. This is because the machine's printing is clear and precise, the process is simple, and one plate can print tens of thousands of sheets. It can also produce colored prints like lithography. Its excellent performance is truly unique in the world. Sales Manager Zhong Yu, recognizing that the current location on Sichuan Road is insufficient, is planning to move to the new company location on Wangping Street.

Yulun Silk and Satin Store's Thriving Business: Yulun Silk and Satin Store, located west of the Nanjing Road Bowling Alley, claims that business has been thriving since its opening the other day. The store is packed with new Chinese and Western silk and satin fabrics, displaying a dazzling array of colors and a complete selection. As a result, shoppers seeking spring clothing have been flocking to the store, and the prices are considered low. Customers have expressed satisfaction. The store holds weekly bargain days every Sunday, offering a flat 10% discount. This is an innovation in the silk and satin industry. Those wishing to purchase silk fabrics during the bargain period can take advantage of this opportunity.

Theater News

The Art Theatre Society Performs for Three Days: The Art Theatre Society has announced that since the news of their second public performance was released, members of the community have been hoping for its early realization. Now, the Society has chosen the 21st, 22nd, and 23rd of this month to perform at the Shanghai Performing Arts Hall, which is run by the Japanese and located on North Sichuan Road. In addition to the selected play "All Quiet on the Western Front" by the German writer Erich Maria Remarque, there will also be a short play "A Zhen" written by the Society's literary department. The meaning is very good. The director will be Ye Chenlu Shi, the lighting will be Shen Duanxian, the set design will be Xu Xingzhi, and the music will be Tao Jingsun. All are experienced people in the art world. When the performance opens, it will definitely be a new and worthwhile offering.

A Grand Comedy Will Be Performed on Stage Alongside the New "Broken Zither Tower" Film: The Star Motion Picture Company has announced that their director, Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu, is an elder statesman in the world of spoken drama, with a solid foundation in dramatic knowledge. The plot of the recently edited film "Broken Zither Tower" is so tragic that others would surely shy away from making such a film. However, Mr. Zheng resolutely took it on, and even the smallest details are conveyed meticulously by Mr. Zheng. Mr. Zheng anticipates that when this film is released, it will surely earn the audience's tears of sympathy. Therefore, he has specially added the hilarious and alluring grand comedy, "The Test of Love," to be performed by Mr. Zheng himself, along with the leading actress, Ms. Hu Die, to harmonize the audience's emotions. They are currently rehearsing day and night, rushing to produce the set design, and will soon meet the audience at the Central Grand Theater.
